<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Our ability to achieve identical supermarket
sales and earnings growth and earnings per share goals may be affected by:
labor disputes, particularly as the Company seeks to manage health care and
pension costs; industry consolidation; pricing and promotional activities of
existing and new competitors, including non-traditional competitors and the
aggressiveness of that competition; our response to these actions; unexpected
changes in product costs; the state of the economy, including interest rates
and the inflationary and deflationary trends in certain commodities; the extent
to which our customers exercise caution in their purchasing behavior in
response to economic conditions; the number of shares outstanding; the success
of our future growth plans; goodwill impairment; volatility in our fuel
margins; and our ability to generate sales at desirable margins, as well as the
success of our programs designed to increase our identical sales without fuel. In
addition, any delays in opening new stores, or changes in the economic climate
could cause us to fall short of our sales and earnings targets.&#160; Our ability to increase identical supermarket
sales also could be adversely affected by increased competition and sales
shifts to other stores that we operate, as well as increases in sales of our
corporate brand products. Earnings and sales also may be affected by adverse
weather conditions, particularly to the extent that hurricanes, tornadoes,
floods, and other conditions disrupt our operations or those of our suppliers;
create shortages in the availability or increases in the cost of products that
we sell in our stores or materials and ingredients we use in our manufacturing
facilities; or raise the cost of supplying energy to our various
operations.&nbsp;Our results also will be affected by the inconsistent pace of
the economic recovery, consumer confidence, and changes in inflation and
deflation in product and operating costs. Our guidance for LIFO is based on our
forecast of cost changes for products in our inventory. Our estimate of product
cost changes could be affected by general economic conditions, weather,
availability of raw materials and ingredients in the products that we sell and
their packaging, and other factors beyond our control. Our non-fuel operating
margin guidance could change if we are unable to pass on any cost increases, if
our strategies fail to deliver the cost savings contemplated, or if changes in
the cost of our inventory and the timing of those changes differ from our
expectations.&#160; Our LIFO charge and the
timing of our recognition of LIFO expense will be affected by changes in
product costs during the year.&nbsp; Our fuel margins could fail to normalize
at 11&#162; per gallon if rapid changes in fuel costs occur.&nbsp; Our capital
expenditures, and the number of projects that we complete, could vary from our
expectations if we are unsuccessful in acquiring suitable sites for new stores;
development costs vary from those budgeted; our logistics and technology or
store projects are not completed on budget or within the time frame projected;
or if current operating conditions fail to improve, or worsen.&#160; Square footage growth during the year is
dependent upon our ability to acquire desirable sites for </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:-1.0in;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Section&nbsp;9 &#151; Financial
Statements and Exhibits</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:-1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:-1.0in;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Item 9.01</font></u><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Financial
Statements and Exhibits.</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:-1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 92.4pt;text-indent:-20.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Exhibits</font></u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 92.4pt;text-indent:-20.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 2.0in;text-indent:-51.6pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">99.1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Earnings
release for second quarter 2010, filed herewith.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5<a name="PB_5_030117_5926"></a></font></p>

</head>

<body lang="EN-US">

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit
99.1</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">KROGER REPORTS STRONG SECOND QUARTER 2010 RESULTS</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Identical Supermarket Sales Increased 2.7%
without Fuel</font></i></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Confirms Fiscal 2010 Guidance</font></i></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">CINCINNATI,
Ohio, September&nbsp;14, 2010 &#151; The Kroger Co. (NYSE: KR) today reported total
sales, which include fuel, increased 6.0% to $18.8 billion in the second
quarter of fiscal 2010 compared with $17.7 billion for the same period last
year.&#160; Excluding fuel sales, total sales
increased 3.3% in the second quarter, which ended August&nbsp;14, 2010, over
the same period last year.&#160; Identical
supermarket sales, without fuel, increased 2.7% in the second quarter over the
same period last year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net earnings for the second quarter totaled $261.6 million, or $0.41
per diluted share.&#160; Net earnings in the
same period last year were $254.4 million, or $0.39 per diluted share.</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;Kroger&#146;s sales have remained solid in the face of competitive and
economic challenges because of the strong credibility we have with our
shoppers.&#160; Our team understands the
importance of finding ways to make each customer visit better than the last
one, resulting in consistent positive identical supermarket sales growth,&#148; said
David B. Dillon, Kroger&#146;s chairman and chief executive officer.&#160; &#147;We continue to build momentum through our
Customer 1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">st</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;strategy, which serves Kroger customers,
associates, shareholders and communities well in a variety of operating
environments.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Details of Second Quarter 2010 Results</font></u></b></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Including Kroger&#146;s retail fuel operations, FIFO gross margin (Table 1)
was 22.51% of sales for the second quarter of fiscal 2010, a decrease of 60
basis points compared to the second quarter last year.&#160; Excluding retail fuel operations, FIFO gross
margin decreased 16 basis points.&#160;
Supermarket selling gross margin (Table 1) declined 12 basis points
without fuel.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1<a name="PB_1_031957_7056"></a></font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='1',FILE='C:\JMS\105981\10-17843-1\task4270348\17843-1-mm.htm',USER='105981',CD='Sep 14 17:51 2010' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kroger recorded an $11.5 million LIFO charge during the quarter, a
decrease of $3.2 million from the same period last year.&#160; Excluding retail fuel sales, the LIFO charge
decreased 2 basis points as a percentage of sales.</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Including Kroger&#146;s retail fuel operations, operating, general and
administrative (OG&amp;A) costs were 17.07% of sales, a decline of 33 basis
points compared with the second quarter last year.&#160; Excluding retail fuel operations, OG&amp;A
increased 7 basis points from the same period last year.</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Financial Strategy</font></u></b></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Capital investment, excluding acquisitions and purchases of leased
facilities, totaled $402.5 million for the second quarter, compared with $518.0
million for the same period last year.</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net total debt (Table 5) was $6.9 billion, a decrease of $393.5 million
from a year ago.&#160; On a rolling
four-quarters basis, Kroger&#146;s net total debt to EBITDA ratio, adjusted for the
southern California impairment charge in fiscal 2009 and Hurricane Ike in
fiscal 2008, was 1.87 compared with 1.77 during the same period last year.</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the second quarter, Kroger invested $148.3 million to repurchase
7.3 million shares of stock at an average price of $20.43 per share.&#160; At the end of the quarter, approximately
$409.2 million remained under the $500 million stock repurchase program
announced in June&nbsp;2010.</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Fiscal 2010 Year-to-Date Results</font></u></b></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the first two quarters of fiscal 2010, total
sales were $43.6 billion compared with $40.5 billion for the same period last
year.&#160; Excluding fuel sales, total sales
increased 3.2% over the prior year.&#160; For
the same period, identical supermarket sales, excluding fuel, increased 2.6%.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2<a name="PB_2_032013_5335"></a></font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='2',FILE='C:\JMS\105981\10-17843-1\task4270348\17843-1-mm.htm',USER='105981',CD='Sep 14 17:51 2010' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net earnings for the first two quarters of fiscal
2010 were $635.3 million or $0.98 per diluted share.&#160; Net earnings for the same period last year
were $689.5 million, or $1.05 per diluted share.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kroger&#146;s operating margin for the first two quarters
of fiscal 2010 decreased 52 basis points as a percentage of sales compared to
the same period last year.&#160; Excluding
retail fuel operations, the Company&#146;s operating margin decreased 57 basis
points as a percentage of sales from the same period last year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Fiscal 2010 Guidance</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kroger confirmed its identical supermarket sales and earnings guidance
for fiscal 2010.&#160; The Company said it continues to expect
identical supermarket sales growth, excluding fuel, of 2% to 3% for the
year.&#160; Net earnings are expected to range
from $1.60 to $1.80 per diluted share for the year.&#160; Kroger still expects to invest approximately
$1.9 to $2.1 billion in capital projects in fiscal 2010.</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;As our results show, we are committed to achieving solid financial
results today while we invest in the future growth of Kroger&#146;s business.&#160; As we move into the second half of the fiscal
year, we are striving to achieve results in the top half of our earnings
guidance range, even as the operating environment remains uncertain,&#148; Mr.&nbsp;Dillon
said.&#160; &#147;Our talented associates are
energized and focused on delivering a great experience in our stores for
shoppers as we enter the holiday season.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="layout-grid-mode:char;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kroger, the nation&#146;s largest
traditional grocery retailer, employs more than 334,000 associates who serve
customers in 2,468 supermarkets and multi-department stores in 31 states under
two dozen local banner names including Kroger, City Market, Dillons, Jay C,
Food 4 Less, Fred Meyer, Fry&#146;s, King Soopers, QFC, Ralphs and Smith&#146;s.&#160; The Company also operates 784 convenience
stores, 372 fine jewelry stores, 932 supermarket fuel centers and 40 food
processing plants in the U.S.&#160; Kroger,
headquartered in Cincinnati, Ohio, focuses its charitable efforts on supporting
hunger </font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3<a name="PB_3_032046_5796"></a></font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>

<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">relief, health and wellness
initiatives, and local organizations in the communities it serves.&#160; For more information about Kroger, please
visit www.kroger.com.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"># # #</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Note:&#160; Fuel sales have historically had low FIFO
gross margin and OG&amp;A rates as compared to corresponding rates on non-fuel
sales.&#160; Additionally, pricing and margins
in Kroger&#146;s retail fuel operations can be volatile on a quarterly basis.&#160; As a result, Kroger discloses such rates,
both including and excluding the effect of retail fuel operations.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This press release contains certain
forward-looking statements about the future performance of the Company.&#160; These statements are based on management&#146;s
assumptions and beliefs in light of the information currently available to
it.&#160; Such statements are indicated by
words such as &#147;confirmed,&#148; &#147;expected,&#148; &#147;expect,&#148;&nbsp;and &#147;achieve.&#148;&#160; Aggressive competition, economic conditions,
interest rates, goodwill impairment, the success of programs designed to
increase our identical supermarket sales without fuel, and labor disputes,
particularly as the Company seeks to manage increases in health care and
pension costs, could materially affect our expected identical supermarket sales
growth and earnings per share, and our goal to achieve results in the top half
of our earnings guidance range. Earnings per share also will be affected by the
number of shares outstanding and volatility in the Company&#146;s fuel margins.&#160; Earnings and sales also may be affected by
adverse weather conditions, particularly to the extent that hurricanes,
tornadoes, floods, and other conditions disrupt our operations or those of our
suppliers; create shortages in the availability or increases in the cost of
products that we sell in our stores or materials and ingredients we use in our
manufacturing facilities; or raise the cost of supplying energy to our various
operations.&#160; Our results also will be
affected by rising commodity costs, the inconsistency of the economic recovery,
consumer confidence, and changes in inflation and deflation in product and
operating costs.&nbsp; Our capital expenditures could vary from our
expectations if we are unsuccessful in acquiring suitable sites for new stores;
development costs vary from those budgeted; our logistics and technology or
store projects are not completed on budget or within the time frame projected;
or if current operating conditions fail to improve, or worsen.&#160; These forward-looking statements are subject
to uncertainties and other factors that could cause actual results to differ
materially.&nbsp; We assume no obligation to update the information contained
herein.&nbsp; Please refer to Kroger&#146;s reports and filings with the Securities
and Exchange Commission for a further discussion of these risks and
uncertainties.</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="1" width="25%" noshade color="black" align="left"></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Note:
Certain prior-year amounts have been reclassified to conform to current-year
presentation.&#160; Certain per share amounts
and percentages may not sum due to rounding.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Note:&#160; The Company defines FIFO gross margin, as
described in the earnings release, as sales minus merchandise costs, including
advertising, warehousing and transportation, but excluding the Last-In
First-Out (LIFO) charge.&#160; This measure is
included to reflect trends in current cost of product.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Note:&#160; The Company defines selling gross margin, as
described in the earnings release related to the Company&#146;s supermarkets, as
gross margin before incurring expenses directly related to distributing and
merchandising the products on its store shelves.&#160; These expenses include advertising,
warehousing, transportation, and shrink.&#160;
Selling gross margin is a measure of how competitively the Company is
pricing the products it sells.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Merchandise costs and
operating, general and administrative expenses exclude depreciation and
amortization expense and rent expense which are included in separate expense
lines.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">LIFO charges of $11.5 and
$14.7 were recorded in the second quarter of 2010 and 2009, respectively.&#160; For the year-to-date period, LIFO charges of
$26.9 and $37.8 were recorded for 2010 and 2009, respectively.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

and comparable supermarket sales are industry-specific measures and it is
important to review them in conjunction with Kroger&#146;s financial results
reported in accordance with GAAP.&#160; Other

differently than Kroger does, limiting the comparability of these measures.</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="1" width="25%" noshade color="black" align="left"></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Kroger defines a
supermarket as identical when it has been open without expansion or relocation
for five full quarters.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Kroger defines a
supermarket as comparable when it has been open for five full quarters,
including expansions and relocations.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Table
5.&#160; Reconciliation of Total Debt to Net
Total Debt</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(in millions)</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(unaudited)</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net
total debt should not be considered an alternative to any GAAP measure of
performance or liquidity.&#160; Management
believes net total debt is an important measure of liquidity, and a primary
component of measuring compliance with the financial covenants under the
Company&#146;s credit facility.&#160; Net total
debt should be reviewed in conjunction with Kroger&#146;s financial results reported
in accordance with GAAP.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

compares the balance in the second quarter of 2010 to the balance in the second
quarter of 2009.</font></p>
